Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Implement Custom Named Folding Regions with Navigation in VS Code

## Objective
Add support for custom named folding regions in VS Code that can be navigated via a quick-pick menu. Users mark regions with special comments (e.g., `// #region MySection` / `// #endregion`), and this feature extends the existing folding to allow naming and jumping to regions by name.

## Requirements

1. **Create a Named Region Provider** in the folding subsystem:
   - Create or extend a folding range provider in `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/`
   - Detect `#region <name>` and `#endregion` comment markers
   - Extract the region name from the marker
   - Register named regions in a data structure that maps name -> line range

2. **Add region decoration** in the editor:
   - Display the region name as a decorative label in the gutter or inline
   - Use VS Code's decoration API (`IModelDecorationOptions`)
   - Collapsed regions should show the name in the fold placeholder text

3. **Register a "Go to Region" command**:
   - Add command `editor.action.goToNamedRegion` in `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/`
   - Wire it to a keybinding (suggest `Ctrl+Shift+R` / `Cmd+Shift+R`)
   - Register the command via `registerEditorAction` or `registerEditorCommand` pattern

4. **Implement quick-pick navigation**:
   - When the command is invoked, show a quick-pick (`IQuickInputService`) listing all named regions in the current file
   - Each item shows the region name and line number
   - Selecting an item navigates the editor cursor to that region and unfolds it

5. **Add a test file** for the named region provider:
   - Test region detection and name extraction
   - Test navigation to a named region

## Key Reference Files
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/folding.ts` — main folding contribution
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/foldingRanges.ts` — FoldingRanges data structure
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/indentRangeProvider.ts` — reference range provider
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/syntaxRangeProvider.ts` — another range provider pattern
- `src/vs/editor/common/model/textModel.ts` — text model API for line access
- `src/vs/editor/contrib/gotoSymbol/browser/goToCommands.ts` — reference for navigation commands
- `src/vs/platform/quickinput/common/quickInput.ts` — QuickInput service interface

## Success Criteria
- Named region detection code exists in folding contrib
- Region name extraction from `#region` markers implemented
- Command registered for navigating to named regions
- Quick-pick integration with region listing
- Decoration or placeholder text shows region names
- Test file exists for the region provider

   544→abstract class FoldingAction<T> extends EditorAction {
   545→
   546→	abstract invoke(foldingController: FoldingController, foldingModel: FoldingModel, editor: ICodeEditor, args: T, languageConfigurationService: ILanguageConfigurationService): void;
   547→
   548→	public override runEditorCommand(accessor: ServicesAccessor, editor: ICodeEditor, args: T): void | Promise<void> {
   549→		const languageConfigurationService = accessor.get(ILanguageConfigurationService);
   550→		const foldingController = FoldingController.get(editor);
   551→		if (!foldingController) {
   552→			return;
   553→		}
   554→		const foldingModelPromise = foldingController.getFoldingModel();
   555→		if (foldingModelPromise) {
   556→			this.reportTelemetry(accessor, editor);
   557→			return foldingModelPromise.then(foldingModel => {
   558→				if (foldingModel) {
   559→					this.invoke(foldingController, foldingModel, editor, args, languageConfigurationService);
   560→					const selection = editor.getSelection();
   561→					if (selection) {
   562→						foldingController.reveal(selection.getStartPosition());
   563→					}
   564→				}
   565→			});
   566→		}
   567→	}
   568→
   569→	protected getSelectedLines(editor: ICodeEditor) {
   570→		const selections = editor.getSelections();
   571→		return selections ? selections.map(s => s.startLineNumber) : [];
   572→	}
   573→
   574→	protected getLineNumbers(args: FoldingArguments, editor: ICodeEditor) {
   575→		if (args && args.selectionLines) {
   576→			return args.selectionLines.map(l => l + 1); // to 0-bases line numbers
   577→		}
   578→		return this.getSelectedLines(editor);
   579→	}
   580→

   582→	}
   583→}

    38→class BitField {
    39→	private readonly _states: Uint32Array;
    40→	constructor(size: number) {
    41→		const numWords = Math.ceil(size / 32);
    42→		this._states = new Uint32Array(numWords);
    43→	}
    44→
    45→	public get(index: number): boolean {
    46→		const arrayIndex = (index / 32) | 0;
    47→		const bit = index % 32;
    48→		return (this._states[arrayIndex] & (1 << bit)) !== 0;
    49→	}

export interface FoldingRange {

	/**
	 * The one-based start line of the range to fold. The folded area starts after the line's last character.
	 */
	start: number;

	/**
	 * The one-based end line of the range to fold. The folded area ends with the line's last character.
	 */
	end: number;

	/**
	 * Describes the {@link FoldingRangeKind Kind} of the folding range such as {@link FoldingRangeKind.Comment Comment} or
	 * {@link FoldingRangeKind.Region Region}. The kind is used to categorize folding ranges and used by commands
	 * like 'Fold all comments'. See
	 * {@link FoldingRangeKind} for an enumeration of standardized kinds.
	 */
	kind?: FoldingRangeKind;
}
export class FoldingRangeKind {
	/**
	 * Kind for folding range representing a comment. The value of the kind is 'comment'.
	 */
	static readonly Comment = new FoldingRangeKind('comment');
	/**
	 * Kind for folding range representing a import. The value of the kind is 'imports'.
	 */
	static readonly Imports = new FoldingRangeKind('imports');
	/**
	 * Kind for folding range representing regions (for example marked by `#region`, `#endregion`).
	 * The value of the kind is 'region'.
	 */
	static readonly Region = new FoldingRangeKind('region');

	/**
	 * Returns a {@link FoldingRangeKind} for the given value.
	 *
	 * @param value of the kind.
	 */
	static fromValue(value: string) {
		switch (value) {
			case 'comment': return FoldingRangeKind.Comment;
			case 'imports': return FoldingRangeKind.Imports;
			case 'region': return FoldingRangeKind.Region;
		}
		return new FoldingRangeKind(value);
	}

	/**
	 * Creates a new {@link FoldingRangeKind}.

## Summary: Quick-Pick UI Integration for Navigation in VS Code

Based on my exploration of the VS Code codebase, here's a comprehensive guide to implementing quick-pick UI for navigation:

### 1. How to Inject and Use IQuickInputService

**Service Injection Pattern:**
```typescript
// In your editor action or contribution
constructor(
  ...other dependencies...,
  @IQuickInputService private readonly quickInputService: IQuickInputService
)
```

**Reference Files:**
- `/workspace/src/vs/platform/quickinput/common/quickInput.ts` - Service interface definition
- `/workspace/src/vs/platform/quickinput/browser/quickInputService.ts` - Service implementation
- `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/indentation/browser/indentation.ts` - Example usage (lines 109-157)

**Service Methods:**
- `pick<T>(picks, options?, token?)` - Show a quick-pick dialog with predefined items
- `input(options?, token?)` - Show text input dialog
- `createQuickPick<T>(options?)` - Create raw IQuickPick for advanced control
- `createInputBox()` - Create raw input box
- `currentQuickInput` - Access currently visible quick input

## Summary: VS Code Folding System

Based on my exploration of the VS Code folding system, here's a comprehensive analysis:

### 1. RangeProvider Interface

**Location:** `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/folding.ts` (lines 48-52)

```typescript
export interface RangeProvider {
    readonly id: string;
    compute(cancelationToken: CancellationToken): Promise<FoldingRegions | null>;
    dispose(): void;
}
```

**Requirements:**
- Must have an `id` property (readonly string) identifying the provider uniquely
- Must implement `compute()` method that returns a Promise resolving to `FoldingRegions` or `null`
- Must implement `dispose()` method for cleanup

### 2. Existing Provider Implementations

There are two main implementations:

#### A. IndentRangeProvider
**Location:** `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/indentRangeProvider.ts`

- **ID:** `'indent'`
- **Purpose:** Calculates folding regions based on indentation levels
- **Key Features:**
  - Uses `computeRanges()` function that analyzes indentation
  - Supports `FoldingMarkers` (regex patterns for `#region`/`#endregion`)
  - Handles off-side rule for languages like Python
  - Implements `RangesCollector` to gather and optimize ranges
  - Respects folding limits with `FoldingLimitReporter`

#### B. SyntaxRangeProvider
**Location:** `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/syntaxRangeProvider.ts`

- **ID:** `'syntax'`
- **Purpose:** Delegates to external `FoldingRangeProvider` instances (language-specific providers)
- **Key Features:**
  - Collects ranges from multiple external providers
  - Validates ranges against document line count
  - Sani

Now let me present the implementation plan for your approval:

## Summary of Implementation Plan

I've designed a **6-phase implementation** to add custom named folding regions with navigation to VS Code:

### Key Design Decisions:

1. **Extend Existing Data Structures**: Add `label?: string` field to `FoldRange` and extend `FoldingRegions` to store labels parallel to start/end indexes

2. **Integrate with IndentRangeProvider**: Extract region names during existing range computation rather than creating a separate provider (simpler, more maintainable)

3. **Add GoToNamedRegionAction**: Create new editor action implementing quick-pick navigation:
   - Shows all named regions in current file
   - Displays region name and line number
   - Navigates to region and unfolds on selection

4. **Optional Decorations**: Display region names in fold placeholders for better UX

### Critical Files:
- `foldingRanges.ts` - Extend FoldRange interface and FoldingRegions class
- `indentRangeProvider.ts` - Extract labels during range computation  
- `folding.ts` - Add GoToNamedRegionAction command
- `namedRegionRangeProvider.test.ts` - Comprehensive tests (NEW)

### Implementation Order:
1. Data structures (low risk)
2. Label extraction in IndentRangeProvider (moderate risk)
3. GoToNamedRegionAction command (moderate risk)
4. Comprehensive tests (high priority)

The plan reuses existing patterns from `gotoSymbolQuickAccess.ts` for the quick-pick UI and `FoldingAction` base class for command registration.

**Ready to proceed with implementation?**

This implementation will:\n\n1. Extract region names from markers (e.g., `// #region MyName` \u2192 store \"MyName\")\n2. Store these names in the folding data structures\n3. Provide a \"Go to Named Region\" command with quick-pick navigation\n4. Display region names in fold decorations\n\n## Analysis Summary\n\nFrom code exploration, the current folding architecture has:\n- **RangeProvider interface**: Implementations compute FoldingRegions from text\n- **FoldingRegions class**: Stores start/end line numbers using Uint32Array, supports types but not names/labels\n- **IndentRangeProvider**: Detects `#region`/`#endregion` markers using regex\n- **EditorActions**: Extend FoldingAction, registered via registerEditorAction()\n- **IQuickInputService**: Provides quick-pick UI for navigation\n\n## Implementation Plan\n\n### Phase 1: Extend Data Structures (LOWER RISK)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/foldingRanges.ts`**\n\n1. Extend `FoldRange` interface:\n   ```typescript\n   export interface FoldRange {\n     // ... existing\n     label?: string;  // Region name extracted from marker\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. Extend `FoldingRegions` class:\n   - Add private `_labels?: Array<string | undefined>` field\n   - Update constructor to accept labels parameter\n   - Add `getLabel(index: number): string | undefined` getter\n   - Update `sanitizeAndMerge()` to merge labels arrays\n\n### Phase 2: Create Named Region Range Provider (MODERATE RISK)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/namedRegionRangeProvider.ts` (NEW)**\n\n1. Create `NamedRegionRangeProvider` class implementing `RangeProvider`\n2. Implement region detection with name extraction:\n   - Parse text to find `#region <name>` and `#endregion` markers\n   - Extract name from marker using regex (handle comments, whitespace)\n   - Support common language patterns: `// #region`, `/* #region */`, `# #region`, etc.\n3. Create labels array parallel to start/end indexes\n4. Return `FoldingRegions` with labels\n\n### Phase 3: Integrate Labels in Existing Providers (MODERATE RISK)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/indentRangeProvider.ts`**\n\nExtend `computeRanges()` function to:\n- Extract labels from `#region <name>` markers when detected\n- Build labels array alongside start/end indexes\n- Pass labels to FoldingRegions constructor\n\n### Phase 4: Register Go-To-Region Command (MODERATE RISK)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/folding.ts`**\n\n1. Create `GoToNamedRegionAction` class extending `FoldingAction`\n2. In `invoke()` method:\n   - Collect all regions with names from foldingModel\n   - Show IQuickInputService picker with region list\n   - On selection: navigate cursor to region, unfold if needed\n3. Register action with ID `editor.action.goToNamedRegion`\n4. Optional: Add keybinding (suggest `Ctrl+Shift+R` / `Cmd+Shift+R`)\n\n### Phase 5: Add Region Label Decorations (LOW RISK - optional enhancement)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/foldingDecorations.ts`**\n\n- Update decorations to show region names in fold placeholders\n- Use IModelDecorationOptions to display labels\n\n### Phase 6: Write Tests (HIGH RISK - must be comprehensive)\n\n**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/test/browser/namedRegionRangeProvider.test.ts` (NEW)**\n\nTest cases:\n1. Region name extraction from `// #region Name`\n2. Nested regions with name preservation\n3. Regions without names (empty `#region`)\n4. Various language comment styles\n5. Navigation to region by name\n6. # Named Folding Regions Implementation Plan

## Context

VS Code currently supports folding regions marked with comments like `// #region` and `// #endregion`, but doesn't capture or use the region names. This implementation will:

1. Extract region names from markers (e.g., `// #region MyName` → store "MyName")
2. Store these names in the folding data structures
3. Provide a "Go to Named Region" command with quick-pick navigation
4. Display region names in fold decorations

## Analysis Summary

From code exploration, the current folding architecture has:
- **RangeProvider interface**: Implementations compute FoldingRegions from text
- **FoldingRegions class**: Stores start/end line numbers using Uint32Array, supports types but not names/labels
- **IndentRangeProvider**: Detects `#region`/`#endregion` markers using regex
- **EditorActions**: Extend FoldingAction, registered via registerEditorAction()
- **IQuickInputService**: Provides quick-pick UI for navigation

## Implementation Plan

### Phase 1: Extend Data Structures (LOWER RISK)

**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/foldingRanges.ts`**

1. Extend `FoldRange` interface:
   ```typescript
   export interface FoldRange {
     // ... existing
     label?: string;  // Region name extracted from marker
   }
   ```

2. Extend `FoldingRegions` class:
   - Add private `_labels?: Array<string | undefined>` field
   - Update constructor to accept labels parameter
   - Add `getLabel(index: number): string | undefined` getter
   - Update `sanitizeAndMerge()` to merge labels arrays

### Phase 2: Create Named Region Range Provider (MODERATE RISK)

**File: `/workspace/src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/browser/namedRegionRangeProvider.ts` (NEW)**

1. Create `NamedRegionRangeProvider` class implementing `RangeProvi
... (truncated)
